## 3. Benchmark Runner Inspection

The benchmark runner is `scripts/pareto_benchmark.py`. It recursively discovers `matrix.csv` when `--root` is a directory, or runs one case when `--root` is a file. The dataset format used by `RiskAwareProblem.from_matrix_csv` is a CSV matrix with an optional header. Lang 3b uses the project-preferred format: `test_id` followed by requirement columns and `0/1` coverage cells.

Important CLI arguments inspected from the runner: `--root`, `--seeds`, `--pop`, `--gens`, `--algorithms`, `--risk-seed`, `--cr-threshold`, `--risk-alpha`, `--archive-size`, `--n-mutants-factor`, `--kill-prob`, and `--output`.

## 10. ROP / Redundancy Analysis

| Algorithm | Feasible entries | Avg ROP | Avg selected_count | Knee objectives | Knee ROP | Knee selected_count | Knee CR |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---|---:|---:|---:|
| ar_qiea | 1347 | 0.767506 | 1123.642910 | `[0.9222423146473779, 0.9957737788425015, 0.43633336093657626]` | 0.732733 | 1062 | 0.972678 |
| mo_qiea | 1089 | 0.771820 | 1126.159780 | `[0.9077757685352622, 0.9919922412031852, 0.4577077107784995]` | 0.724684 | 1085 | 0.950820 |
| nsga2 | 529 | 0.774971 | 1041.315690 | `[0.9439421338155516, 0.996782769588788, 0.410566034582576]` | 0.756131 | 993 | 0.978142 |
| random_front | 722 | 0.828953 | 1841.124654 | `[0.9005424954792043, 0.9925631123250643, 0.3227248477876231]` | 0.788707 | 1454 | 0.950820 |

ROP is diagnostic only. Lower ROP generally means the selected tests overlap less on the same covered requirements. On this dataset, random_front tends to produce lower redundancy because random density sampling often selects smaller subsets. AR-QIEA and MO-QIEA produce larger fronts and stronger HV, but their selected subsets are usually larger and therefore more redundant than the random baseline.

## 11. Statistical Analysis

| Comparison | AR-QIEA wins | AR-QIEA losses | Ties | Wilcoxon p-value |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---|
| ar_qiea vs mo_qiea | 22 | 8 | 0 | None |
| ar_qiea vs nsga2 | 28 | 2 | 0 | None |
| ar_qiea vs random_front | 30 | 0 | 0 | None |

P1 gate result: **INCONCLUSIVE - mean HV condition passed, p-values unavailable because SciPy is missing**.

Mean HV condition:

- AR-QIEA mean HV = `0.428521`
- MO-QIEA mean HV = `0.416320`
- Random front mean HV = `0.252479`

The mean HV condition is satisfied, but the statistical p-value condition cannot be evaluated in this environment because SciPy is missing and the benchmark therefore wrote `null` Wilcoxon values.

## 12. Detailed Interpretation

- Best mean HV: `ar_qiea`.
- Largest average Pareto front: `ar_qiea`.
- Best mean MSR: `random_front`.
- Best mean CGCC: `random_front`.
- Best mean ETR: `ar_qiea`.
- Fastest mean runtime: `random_front`.
- Runtime trade-off: AR-QIEA produced the strongest mean HV and largest front, but it was much slower than NSGA-II and random_front. MO-QIEA was also slow and had lower mean HV than AR-QIEA, supporting the risk-adaptive contribution direction at the mean-metric level.
- Paper-claim support: the Lang 3b run supports the directional HV claim by mean value, but it is not fully paper-ready because the Wilcoxon p-values were unavailable. A rerun after installing SciPy, or a post-run p-value computation with SciPy, is needed for the p < 0.05 claim.
- Dataset limitation: 2,158 of 2,245 tests have no coverage against the modified-line requirements. This sparsity affects ETR and redundancy behavior because many selected tests may add execution cost without improving CR/MSR/CGCC.
- Synthetic-risk limitation: MSR, CGCC, and execution time use P1 synthetic/proxy risk settings, not real Major mutation or real call-graph centrality.

## 13. Error / Warning Log

- The clean benchmark passed with exit code 0.
- Before the clean run, duplicate interrupted benchmark processes were found and stopped to prevent output-file races. No dataset content was changed.
- SciPy is not installed in the project virtual environment, so Wilcoxon p-values are unavailable and appear as `null` in the JSON.
- Per-seed runtime values are not persisted by `scripts/pareto_benchmark.py`; only aggregate runtime statistics are available.
- Dataset sparsity warning: `2158` empty test rows.
- No malformed matrix cells, duplicate tests, duplicate requirements, width errors, or metadata count inconsistencies were found.
- No traceback occurred during the clean benchmark. Benchmark log content:

```text
{
  "output": "artifacts\\pareto\\lang3b_full_19-06-2026.json",
  "cases": 1
}
```

## 14. Reproduction Commands

Run from project root:

```powershell
cd "D:\FPT\Study\2026\sem5\SWT301\Quantun+Testing\OFFICIAL\quantum-testing"
$env:PYTHONPATH='src'
D:\FPT\Study\2026\sem5\SWT301\Quantun+Testing\OFFICIAL\.venv\Scripts\python.exe -m pytest -q tests\test_metrics_mo.py tests\test_risk_problem.py tests\test_ar_qiea.py tests\test_nsga2.py
```
